/****** Object:  View [dbo].[View_1]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[View_1]
AS
SELECT dbo.employee.employeeName, dbo.employee.employeePosition, dbo.PunishTypes.PunishName, dbo.rooms.roomName, dbo.Punish.punishText
FROM     dbo.employee INNER JOIN
                  dbo.Punish ON dbo.employee.ID = dbo.Punish.empID INNER JOIN
                  dbo.PunishTypes ON dbo.Punish.punshType = dbo.PunishTypes.ID INNER JOIN
                  dbo.rooms ON dbo.employee.room_id = dbo.rooms.ID
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ALlreports]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ALlreports]
AS
BEGIN
	SELECT 
  dbo.Punish.punishText,
  dbo.Punish.punishDate,
  dbo.Punish.ID,
  dbo.employee.employeeName,
  dbo.employee.employeePosition,
  dbo.employee.cid,
  dbo.rooms.roomName,
  dbo.Subjects.subjectName,
  dbo.roomlagna.lagna_no,
  dbo.PunishTypes.PunishName
FROM
((((  dbo.employee
  INNER JOIN dbo.Punish ON (dbo.employee.ID = dbo.Punish.empID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.rooms ON (dbo.Punish.roomID = dbo.rooms.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.Subjects ON (dbo.Punish.SubjectID = dbo.Subjects.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.roomlagna ON (dbo.Punish.lagnaID = dbo.roomlagna.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.PunishTypes ON (dbo.Punish.punshType = dbo.PunishTypes.ID)
  /* Procedure body */
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[employee_I]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[employee_I]
  
  @employeeName nvarchar(200),
  @cid float,
  @fileno float,
  @employeePosition nvarchar(150),
  @room_id float,
  @roomName nvarchar(150)
AS
BEGIN

DECLARE @ID INT;

if not EXISTS (select * from employee where cid=@cid)
BEGIN
  INSERT INTO
    dbo.employee
  (
    
    employeeName,
    cid,
    fileno,
    employeePosition,
    room_id,
    roomName
  )
  VALUES (
   
    @employeeName,
    @cid,
    @fileno,
    @employeePosition,
    @room_id,
    @roomName
  )
  SELECT ID,employeeName FROM employee WHERE (ID = SCOPE_IDENTITY())
  set @ID=SCOPE_IDENTITY()
  
     RETURN @ID
  
  end 
  
  ELSE
  BEGIN
  set @ID=(select ID from employee where cid=@cid)
  UPDATE employee set room_id=@room_id,roomName=@roomName  where cid=@cid
  RETURN @ID
  
  end 
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[procedure1]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[procedure1]
@id int
AS
BEGIN
SELECT dbo.employee.ID, dbo.Punish.lagnaID, dbo.Punish.punshType, dbo.Punish.punishText, dbo.Punish.SubjectID, dbo.Punish.punishDate, dbo.rooms.roomName, dbo.employee.employeeName, dbo.employee.cid, dbo.PunishTypes.PunishName, 
                  dbo.PunishTypes.ID AS Expr1
FROM     dbo.employee INNER JOIN
                  dbo.Punish ON dbo.employee.ID = dbo.Punish.empID INNER JOIN
                  dbo.rooms ON dbo.Punish.roomID = dbo.rooms.ID INNER JOIN
                  dbo.PunishTypes ON dbo.Punish.punshType = dbo.PunishTypes.ID
                  where  dbo.employee.ID=@id
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Punish_Insert]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Punish_Insert]
 
  @empID int,
  @roomID int,
  @lagnaID int,
  @punshType int,
  @punishText nvarchar(max),
  @SubjectID int,
  @punishDate date
  
AS
BEGIN
DECLARE @ID INT;
if not EXISTS(select * from dbo.Punish where empID=@empID and punishDate=@punishDate)
begin  
 INSERT INTO
    dbo.Punish
  (
    empID,
    roomID,
    lagnaID,
    punshType,
    punishText,
    SubjectID,
    punishDate
  )
  VALUES (
    
    @empID,
    @roomID,
    @lagnaID,
    @punshType,
    @punishText,
    @SubjectID,
    @punishDate
  )
  
  SELECT ID,empID FROM Punish WHERE (ID = SCOPE_IDENTITY())
  set @ID=SCOPE_IDENTITY()
  
     RETURN @ID
end 
else 
begin
  
   set @ID=(select ID from  dbo.Punish   where empID=@empID and punishDate=@punishDate and punshType=@punshType);
   UPDATE
    dbo.Punish
  SET
    empID = @empID,
    roomID = @roomID,
    lagnaID = @lagnaID,
    punshType = @punshType,
    punishText = @punishText,
    SubjectID = @SubjectID,
    punishDate = @punishDate
  WHERE
    ID = @ID
   RETURN @ID
end 
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PunishProc]    Script Date: 1/25/2022 8:03:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PunishProc]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@id int
AS
BEGIN
	SELECT 
  dbo.Punish.punishText,
  dbo.Punish.punishDate,
  dbo.Punish.ID,
  dbo.employee.employeeName,
  dbo.employee.employeePosition,
  dbo.employee.cid,
  dbo.rooms.roomName,
  dbo.Subjects.subjectName,
  dbo.roomlagna.lagna_no,
  dbo.PunishTypes.PunishName
FROM
((((  dbo.employee
  INNER JOIN dbo.Punish ON (dbo.employee.ID = dbo.Punish.empID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.rooms ON (dbo.Punish.roomID = dbo.rooms.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.Subjects ON (dbo.Punish.SubjectID = dbo.Subjects.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.roomlagna ON (dbo.Punish.lagnaID = dbo.roomlagna.ID))
  INNER JOIN dbo.PunishTypes ON (dbo.Punish.punshType = dbo.PunishTypes.ID)
where  dbo.Punish.ID=@id

END
GO
